==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// failure case
package xxx;
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2
```


package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
```java
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null) {
                String varName = varAccess.getName();
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParents()
                    .first(ASTBlock.class)
                    .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getName().equals(varName));

                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null) {
                String variableName = variableAccess.getName();
                List<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParentsOfType(ASTBlock.class)
                    .get(0)
                    .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                    .filter(expr -> {
                        ASTVariableAccess access = expr.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        return access != null && access.getName().equals(variableName);
                    })
                    .toList();

                if (assignments.size() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression rightOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (rightOperand != null && rightOperand.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftHandSide = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftHandSide != null && leftHandSide.getType() != null && leftHandSide.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftHandSide = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (leftHandSide != null && leftHandSide.getType() != null && leftHandSide.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass("java.lang.String")) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getSymbol().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass("java.lang.String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        assignments.forEach(assignment -> visit(assignment, data));
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        assignments.forEach(assignment -> visit(assignment, data));
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass(String.class)) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpr = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpr != null && infixExpr.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUAL || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.EQUAL) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClassOrInterfaceType("java.lang.String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return data;
    }
}

```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
```

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

```
import java.util.*;

        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
```

```java
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;
```

        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override

        if (node.getOperator() == JavaToken.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && "description".equals(variableAccess.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_EQUALS || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftHandSide = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftHandSide != null && leftHandSide.getType() != null && leftHandSide.getType().isClassType("java.lang.String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
    public void bad() {
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getSymbol().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (node.getMethodName().equals("append") && node.getFirstChild() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getFirstChild();
            if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getSymbol().getName().equals("StringBuilder")) {
                return super.visit(node, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String field in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    private String logStatement = "";

    public void bad() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }

    public void good() {
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {
            sb.append(val).append(", ");
        }
        logStatement = sb.toString();
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 9
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void addViolation(Object data, JavaNode node) {
        addViolation(data, node, "Avoid using '+=' or '+' for String concatenation in loops. Use StringBuilder or StringBuffer instead.");
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isClass(String.class)) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```java
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == AssignmentOperator.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {

                }
```

```java
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 11
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTBlock block = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
                if (block != null) {
                    NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                            .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN)
                            .filter(expr -> {
                                ASTVariableAccess va = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                                return va != null && va.getType() != null && va.getType().isString();
                            });
                    if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 11
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                ASTBlock block = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
                if (block != null) {
                    NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = block.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                            .filter(expr -> expr.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT)
                            .filter(expr -> {
                                ASTVariableAccess va = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                                return va != null && va.getType() != null && va.getType().isString() && va.getName().equals(variableAccess.getName());
                            });
                    if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
